# KINGBOT FALLBACK MD5 400KB TXT ALGORITHM
# Thuật toán thật ưu tiên add ở Admin HTML. File TXT này chỉ là dự phòng khi admin code trống/lỗi.
# Output chuẩn: dict taixiu, tx_conf, dice, total, chanle, risk, trend, details.

def _hex_bytes(md5):
    s = str(md5).lower().strip()
    if len(s) != 32:
        return []
    try:
        return [int(s[i:i+2], 16) for i in range(0,32,2)]
    except Exception:
        return []

def _nibbles(md5):
    try:
        return [int(c,16) for c in str(md5).lower().strip()]
    except Exception:
        return []

def _pick_cau(md5, b, n, gate='', level='basic'):
    patterns = []
    left = sum(b[:8]); right = sum(b[8:])
    odd = sum(x for i,x in enumerate(n) if i % 2); even = sum(x for i,x in enumerate(n) if not i % 2)
    mirror = sum(abs(n[i]-n[31-i]) for i in range(16))
    runs = []
    cur = 1
    for i in range(1, len(n)):
        if (n[i] >= 8) == (n[i-1] >= 8): cur += 1
        else:
            runs.append(cur); cur = 1
    runs.append(cur)
    maxrun = max(runs) if runs else 1
    if maxrun >= 5: patterns.append('Cầu bệt dài')
    if maxrun == 4: patterns.append('Cầu bệt 4 nhịp')
    if sum(1 for i in range(1,len(n)) if (n[i]>=8)!=(n[i-1]>=8)) >= 22: patterns.append('Cầu đảo 1-1')
    if sum(1 for i in range(2,len(n)) if (n[i]>=8)==(n[i-2]>=8) and (n[i]>=8)!=(n[i-1]>=8)) >= 12: patterns.append('Cầu nhịp 2-2')
    if abs(left-right) < 80: patterns.append('Cầu cân bằng')
    if abs(left-right) > 350: patterns.append('Cầu lệch biên')
    if mirror < 65: patterns.append('Cầu mirror')
    if mirror > 145: patterns.append('Cầu gãy mirror')
    if abs(odd-even) < 35: patterns.append('Cầu chẵn/lẻ cân')
    if abs(odd-even) > 160: patterns.append('Cầu chẵn/lẻ lệch')
    pairs = sum(1 for i in range(0,31,2) if n[i] == n[i+1])
    if pairs >= 5: patterns.append('Cầu pair/song thủ')
    if n[0] in (0,15) or n[-1] in (0,15): patterns.append('Biên cực trị')
    if abs(sum(n[:16]) - sum(n[16:])) <= 10: patterns.append('Sát nút 10-11')
    if not patterns: patterns.append('Cầu hỗn hợp hash')
    return patterns[:5]

def _core(md5, gate='', level='basic'):
    s = str(md5).lower().strip()
    b = _hex_bytes(s); n = _nibbles(s)
    if not b or not n:
        return None
    salt = ('KINGBOT-TXT-400KB|' + str(gate) + '|' + str(level) + '|' + s).encode()
    h1 = hashlib.sha256(salt).digest()
    h2 = hashlib.sha512(salt + h1).digest()
    hb = list(h1 + h2)
    left = sum((i+3)*(b[i] ^ hb[i]) for i in range(16))
    right = sum((19-i)*(b[i] + hb[31-i]) for i in range(16))
    nib = sum((i+5)*(n[i] + hb[i] % 16) for i in range(32))
    mirror = sum((i+1)*abs(n[i]-n[31-i]) for i in range(16))
    xorv = 0
    for i,x in enumerate(b): xorv ^= ((x << (i % 5)) & 255) ^ hb[i]
    entropy = int(statistics.pstdev(b) * 100) if len(b) > 1 else 0
    wave = (left*31 + right*17 + nib*13 + mirror*11 + xorv*29 + entropy*7) % 100000
    gate_bias = sum(ord(c) for c in str(gate)) % 97
    level_bias = {'free': 11, 'basic': 23, 'pro': 37}.get(str(level), 19)
    raw = (wave + gate_bias*41 + level_bias*73 + hb[5]*17 + hb[44]*9) % 10000
    score = raw / 100.0
    d1 = ((b[0] + hb[0] + wave) % 6) + 1
    d2 = ((b[7] ^ hb[7] ^ xorv) % 6) + 1
    d3 = ((b[15] + hb[15] + mirror + nib) % 6) + 1
    total = d1 + d2 + d3
    # Tổng mô phỏng cũng được hòa với score để bắt các dạng cầu cao/thấp, chẵn/lẻ, bệt/đảo.
    if score >= 50:
        tx = 'TÀI'
        if total < 11:
            d3 = min(6, d3 + (11-total)); total = d1+d2+d3
    else:
        tx = 'XỈU'
        if total > 10:
            d3 = max(1, d3 - (total-10)); total = d1+d2+d3
    cau = _pick_cau(s, b, n, gate, level)
    dist = abs(score-50)
    conf = min(98, max(53, 56 + int(dist*0.75) + (len(cau) % 6)))
    if level == 'free': conf = min(conf, 82)
    if level == 'pro': conf = min(99, conf + 4)
    risk_point = int((entropy/35 + mirror/9 + abs(raw-5000)/88 + xorv/5) % 100)
    risk = 'THẤP' if risk_point < 35 else ('TRUNG BÌNH' if risk_point < 70 else 'CAO')
    risk_emoji = '🟢' if risk == 'THẤP' else ('🟡' if risk == 'TRUNG BÌNH' else '🔴')
    trend = ' / '.join(cau)
    return {
        'engine': 'TXT-DỰ-PHÒNG-MD5-400KB ALL-CAU',
        'taixiu': tx,
        'tx_conf': conf,
        'chanle': 'CHẴN' if total % 2 == 0 else 'LẺ',
        'dice': f'{d1}-{d2}-{d3}',
        'total': total,
        'risk': risk,
        'risk_emoji': risk_emoji,
        'score': round(score, 2),
        'hash_short': s[:8].upper() + '...' + s[-6:].upper(),
        'trend': trend,
        'details': cau + ['cao/thấp', 'chẵn/lẻ', 'entropy MD5']
    }

def predict(md5, gate='', level='basic'):
    return _core(md5, gate, level)

def predict_basic(md5, gate='', level='basic'):
    return _core(md5, gate, 'basic')

def predict_pro(md5, gate='', level='pro'):
    return _core(md5, gate, 'pro')

def predict_free(md5, gate='', level='free'):
    return _core(md5, gate, 'free')
